
#=========================ESCORT

fleet "MGF: Escort Huge" 
	government "Merchant"
		names "civilian"
		cargo 4
		personality
			confusion 30
			timid appeasing
	variant 50
		"CH-6 Carrack"
	variant 50
		"CDB-6K Jupiter"
	variant 30
		"FPd45 Clinker"
	variant 30
		"FAd36 Flint"
	variant 40
		"FUe02a Gebrant"
	variant 40
		"FUe04a Gebrant II"

mission "MGF: Escort (Huge 1, Dangerous Destination)"
	name "Escort to <planet>"
	description "The captain of the <npc> will pay you <payment> to escort them safely into a dangerous region of space to reach <destination> by <date>."
	repeat
	job
	deadline 10
	to offer
		random < 15
		"combat rating" > 100
	source
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent"
		#attributes "deep" "paradise" "near earth"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent"
		attributes "frontier"
		distance 3 6
	npc
		government "Pirate"
		personality nemesis harvests plunders
		system destination
		fleet "Small Northern Pirates"
		fleet "Small Northern Pirates"
		fleet "Large Northern Pirates"
	npc
		government "Pirate"
		personality nemesis entering harvests plunders
		system destination
		fleet "Large Northern Pirates"
	npc
		government "Pirate"
		personality nemesis staying harvests plunders
		system destination
		fleet "Small Northern Pirates"
		fleet "Large Northern Pirates"
	
	npc accompany save
		government "Merchant"
		personality escort timid
		fleet "MGF: Escort Huge" 
		#fleet
		#	names "civilian"
		#	variant
		#		"CH-6 Carrack"
	on complete
		payment 350000
		dialog phrase "generic safe escort completion dialog"
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic arrived-without-npc dialog"

#=========================Canaveral Naval Yard

mission "MGF CNY: Large Construction Supplies [0]"
	name "Large rush delivery to <planet>"
	job
	repeat
	deadline 30
	description "A large construction project at <destination> requires a lot of materials, deliver <cargo> to <destination> by <date>. Payment is <payment>."
	cargo "Construction Supplies" 200 600
	to offer
		has "event: mgf: canaveral naval yard begin"
		not "event: mgf: canaveral naval yard done"
		random < 40 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
	source
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing"
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
	destination
		distance 3 16
		planet "Canaveral Naval Yard"
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on complete
		payment
		payment 600000
		"mgf: canaveral construction assist" += 1
		dialog phrase "generic cargo delivery payment"

#=========================Navy

mission "MGF: Navy Targeted Surveillance"
	name "Scan Target Ship"
	description "The <npc>, a ship owned by NGK, is about to enter this system. Intercept it and make detailed scans of its cargo for Navy Intelligence on <destination>; proceed there before <date> for <payment> after retrieving the data."
	job
	deadline 1 7
	repeat
	to offer
		random < 10
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Hauling" >= 1
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Security" >= 1
		"reputation: MGF: Republic" >= 1
	source
		government Republic Neutral
	destination
		government Republic
		attributes military
		distance 1 5
	npc "scan cargo"
		government "MGF: NGK Hauling"
		personality fleeing uninterested entering target
		fleet
			names "ngk name"
			variant 4
				"Nasprite (NGK Secure Cargo)"
			variant
				"E-VC14 Zuiho (Secure Cargo)"
				"Xencar (NGK)" 6
		dialog "You manage to make the requested scans of the <npc>'s cargo. Time to head to <planet>."
	on complete
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Security" -= 1
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Security" >?= 0
		"reputation: MGF: Republic" += 1
		"mgf: assisted navy" += 1
		dialog `You transmit your scans and receive you payment of <payment>. The Navy officer quickly thanks you and immediately cut the comms.`
		payment 92000

#===========================Nordlin Navy Yard

mission "MGF NNY: Large Construction Supplies [0]"
	name "Large rush delivery to <planet>"
	job
	repeat
	deadline 30
	description "Major upgrade is being done to Nordlin Navy Yard which requires <cargo>. Deliver it to <destination> by <date>. Payment is <payment>."
	cargo "Construction Supplies" 200 600
	to offer
		has "event: mgf: nordlin navy yard upgrade begin"
		not "event: mgf: nordlin navy yard upgrade done"
		random < 40 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
	source
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing"
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
	destination
		distance 3 14
		planet "Nordlin Navy Yard"
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on complete
		payment
		payment 300000
		dialog phrase "generic cargo delivery payment"

#=====================Vinci
#export, vacuum research, station research, build station.

mission "MGF: CPU Export"
	name "Export to <planet>"
	job
	repeat
	deadline 30
	description "Deliver <cargo> to <destination> by <date>. Payment is <payment>."
	cargo "CPU" 30 50
	to offer
		random < 30 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
		#Probably want something decently tough to carry such valuable cargo, not just any Star Barges.
		or
			"flagship attribute: hull" > 4000 * 1000
			"flagship attribute: shields" > 3000 * 1000 # * 1000 as values returned are x1000 of the data, see ES wiki for info.
	source
		attributes "electronics export" "processor export"
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
	destination
		distance 3 16
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes "medium factory" "large factory"
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on complete
		payment 50000 2500
		dialog phrase "generic cargo delivery payment"

#Research mission requiring heavy ship as stable platform
mission "MGF: Vinci Vacuum Research"
	name "Research Project"
	job
	repeat
	deadline 30
	description "Transport <cargo> and <bunks> of researchers to <waypoint> and back by <date>. Payment is <payment>. To accept you need a ship heavier than 2000 tons for stability."
	cargo "Research Instruments" 100
	passengers 12
	to offer
		random < 30 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
		"MGF: CPU Export: done" >= 3
		"armament deterrence" > 5
		not "mgf: vinci station research phase 1 done"
	to accept
		"flagship attribute: mass" > 2000 * 1000
	source
		attributes "electronics export" "processor export"
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		planet "Vinci"
	waypoint
		distance 2 5
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on complete
		payment 150000 2700
		dialog phrase "generic cargo delivery payment"

mission "MGF: Vinci Station Research Phase 1"
	landing
	invisible
	to offer
		or
			"MGF: Vinci Vacuum Research: done" >= 3
			"year" >= 3020
	on offer
		"mgf: vinci station research phase 1 done" = 1
		fail

mission "MGF: Vinci Station Tour"
	name "Researcher transport to <planet>"
	job
	description "Bring <bunks> researchers to <stopovers> for a meeting and back. Payment is <payment>."
	passengers 3
	source
		attributes "electronics export" "processor export"
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		planet "Vinci"
	stopover "EB-1A Forge Station"
	to offer
		not "mgf: vinci station research phase 2 done"
		"armament deterrence" > 4
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic passenger on visit"
	on stopover
		dialog
			`You docked at the station and shortly after the researchers left your ship to go to their meeting. They return after a few hours and repare to leave. You hear them talking about space and how very few industries ever consider the benefits of it and even fewer took advantage of it, as if most of humanity collectively forget about possible use of space stations beyond refineries and shipyards for a good portion of the millennium.`
	on complete
		payment
		payment 8000
		event "mgf: vinci hoerni station construction begin" 360
		dialog phrase "generic passenger dropoff payment"

mission "MGF: Vinci Station Research Phase 2"
	landing
	invisible
	to offer
		"MGF: Vinci Station Tour: done" <= 0
		"year" >= 3021
	on offer
		event "mgf: vinci hoerni station construction begin" 360
		fail

planet "MGF: Fake Vinci"
	government "MGF: Fake Planets"
	attributes "requires: unlandable" "requires: sdfksdfo"
	description `If you can land here its a bug.`

planet "Nt24 Hoerni Station"
	attributes station research #add export later.
	landscape "land/station23"
	description `A large station owned by Selcon Corporation for research and manufacturing electronic chips especially various kind of processors taking various advantage of micro-gravitiy environment to decrease defects resulting in higher quality products in higher quantity.`
	description `Currently the facilities on the station are being tested and with limited production mostly for research purpose. Though, it is estimated that once the station goes into full production it can rival multiple planetary fabrication plants combined.`
	spaceport `Like most other part on the station, the port is very clean and painted in white. There's very few basic ameneties available and most other area are off-limits for visitors.`

event "mgf: vinci hoerni station construction begin"
	system Miaplacidus
		add object "MGF: Fake Vinci"
			distance 274.75
			period 85.8737
			object "Nt24 Hoerni Station"
				sprite "planet/mgf hoerni station 50"
				offset 180
				distance 167
				period 20.3008

mission "MGF: Vinci Station Construction Complete"
	landing
	invisible
	to offer
		has "event: mgf: vinci hoerni station construction begin"
	on offer
		event "mgf: vinci hoerni station construction done" 360
		fail

event "mgf: vinci hoerni station construction done"
	"mgf: hoerni station post 23012024 patch" = 1
	system Miaplacidus
		remove object "MGF: Fake Vinci"
			distance 274.75
			period 85.8737
			object "Nt24 Hoerni Station"
				sprite "planet/mgf hoerni station 50"
				offset 180
				distance 167
				period 20.3008
		add object "MGF: Fake Vinci"
			distance 274.75
			period 85.8737
			object "Nt24 Hoerni Station"
				sprite "planet/mgf hoerni station"
				offset 180
				distance 167
				period 20.3008
	planet "Nt24 Hoerni Station"
		attributes station research "electronics export" "processor export"
		landscape "land/station23"
		description `A large station owned by Selcon Corporation for research and manufacturing electronic chips especially various kind of processors taking various advantage of micro-gravitiy environment to decrease defects resulting in higher quality products in higher quantity.`
		description `With the testing phase completed the station manufacturing is running at full capacity completely overtaking.`
		spaceport `Like most other part on the station, the port is very clean and painted in white. There's very few basic ameneties available and most other area are off-limits for visitors.`

event "mgf: hoerni station sprite patch"
	system Miaplacidus
		remove object "MGF: Fake Vinci"
		add object "MGF: Fake Vinci"
			distance 274.75
			period 85.8737
			object "Nt24 Hoerni Station"
				sprite "planet/mgf hoerni station"
				offset 180
				distance 167
				period 20.3008

mission "MGF: Hoerni Station Sprite Patch"
	landing
	invisible
	to offer
		has "event: mgf: vinci hoerni station construction done"
		not "event: mgf: hoerni station sprite patch"
		not "mgf: hoerni station post 20240123 patch"
	on offer
		event "mgf: hoerni station sprite patch"
		fail

mission "MGF: EB-1A Forge Gas Import (Hydrogen 1)"
	name "Gas Transport to <planet>"
	description "4000 units of Liquid Hydrogen along with <cargo> to confirm the batch is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>."
	job
	repeat
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		random < 50
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "oil"
	destination
		planet "EB-1A Forge Station"
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 3 20
	on offer
		require "M-type 1k Gas Tank" 2
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): M-type 1k Gas Tank" >= 2 + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Natural Gas" / 2000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Ethane" / 2000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Hydrogen" / 2000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Liquid Hydrogen" 4000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Liquid Hydrogen" -4000
	on complete
		outfit "Liquid Hydrogen" -4000
		dialog "You were directed to a special dock for transferring liquid gas and begin the discharging process. <payment> is transferred into your account after it finishes."
		payment 1250000 17000

mission "MGF: EB-1A Forge Chem Import (Hydrochloric 1)"
	name "Chemical Transport to <planet>"
	description "2000 units of Hydrochloric Acid along with <cargo> to confirm the validity is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>. To accept this job you need flagship capable of carrying highly corrosive chemical."
	job
	repeat
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		random < 60
		has "outfit (flagship installed): U-type 1k Chemical Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "medium factory" "large factory"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		planet "EB-1A Forge Station"
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): U-type 1k Chemical Tank" >= 2 + ( "outfit (installed): Sulfuric Acid" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Phosphoric Acid" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Methanol" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Ammonia" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Hydrazine" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Diborane" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Chlorine" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Hydrochloric Acid" / 1000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Hydrochloric Acid" 2000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Hydrochloric Acid" -2000
	on complete
		outfit "Hydrochloric Acid" -2000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload chemical station"
		payment 500000 12000

	name "Large dry bulk delivery to <planet>"
	job
	repeat
	description "Deliver <cargo> to <destination>. Payment is <payment>."
	cargo "coke types" 500 2000 
	to offer
		random < 60
		"cargo space" > 500
		or
			has "flagship attributes: bulk bay"
			has "ship model: CDB-6K Jupiter"
			has "ship model: CDB-12K Saturn"
			has "ship model: Bulk Freighter"
			has "ship model: SV80-n Catirfel"
			has "ship model: SV40-n Navilel"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Bulk Cargo Bay"
	source
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes mining oil
	destination
		attributes "mgf: large refinery station"
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on complete
		payment
		payment 5000
		dialog phrase "generic cargo delivery payment"

mission "MGF: Large Refinery Station Gas Import (Hydrogen 1)"
	name "Gas Transport to <planet>"
	description "4000 units of Liquid Hydrogen along with <cargo> to confirm the batch is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>."
	job
	repeat
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		random < 50
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "oil"
	destination
		attributes "mgf: large refinery station"
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 3 20
	on offer
		require "M-type 1k Gas Tank" 2
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): M-type 1k Gas Tank" >= 2 + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Natural Gas" / 2000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Ethane" / 2000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Hydrogen" / 2000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Liquid Hydrogen" 4000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Liquid Hydrogen" -4000
	on complete
		outfit "Liquid Hydrogen" -4000
		dialog "You were directed to a special dock for transferring liquid gas and begin the discharging process. <payment> is transferred into your account after it finishes."
		payment 1250000 17000

mission "MGF: Large Refinery Station Chem Import (Hydrochloric 1)"
	name "Chemical Transport to <planet>"
	description "2000 units of Hydrochloric Acid along with <cargo> to confirm the validity is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>. To accept this job you need flagship capable of carrying highly corrosive chemical."
	job
	repeat
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		random < 60
		has "outfit (flagship installed): U-type 1k Chemical Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "medium factory" "large factory"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes "mgf: large refinery station"
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): U-type 1k Chemical Tank" >= 2 + ( "outfit (installed): Sulfuric Acid" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Phosphoric Acid" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Methanol" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Ammonia" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Hydrazine" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Diborane" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Chlorine" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Hydrochloric Acid" / 1000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Hydrochloric Acid" 2000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Hydrochloric Acid" -2000
	on complete
		outfit "Hydrochloric Acid" -2000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload chemical station"
		payment 500000 12000

mission "MGF: Hire Small Crossguard Escort"
	name "Hire Small Crossguard Escort"
	job
	repeat
	deadline 30
	description `Hire a small fleet of Crossguard warships to escort you for 1 month (<date>). You will pay 480,000 credits upfront for the escort with no further fees.`
	to offer
		or
			random < 30
			#-----Higher chance if using freighter with no escorts.
			and
				random < 50
				or
					has "ship: Light Freighter"
					has "ship: Heavy Freighter"
				"ship: Interceptor" < 3
				"ship: Light Warship" < 3
				"ship: Medium Warship" < 2
				"ship: Heavy Warship" < 1
	source
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent"
		attributes "dirt belt" rim "south"
	on accept
		payment -480000
	
	npc
		government "Escort" #So they attack everything that attack you.
		personality
			confusion 20
			hunting disables
		fleet
			names "crossguard name"
			variant 6
				"Marauder Quicksilver (XGS Escort)" 4
			variant 4
				"Marauder Quicksilver (XGS Escort, Weapons)" 4
	on fail
		dialog
			`The captain of <npc> informs you that they've completed the 1 month contract and give you a farewell.`
	to complete
		never

	name "Arrest Corporate Saboteur"
	description `A saboteur was identified to be escaping in a transport named <npc>, disable and board it to arrest the saboteur and bring the to <origin> and receive your payment of <payment>. To accept you need a Brig.`
	deadline 5
	repeat
	job
	to offer
		random < 15
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Hauling" >= 3
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Security" >= 3
	source
		government Republic Syndicate "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes core
		attributes urban
	to accept
		has "outfit (flagship installed): Brig"
	
	npc board
		government "Bounty"
		personality launching target fleeing uninterested
		system
			distance 0 0
		fleet
			names "civilian"
			variant
				"Arrow"
			variant
				"Shuttle"
			variant
				"Heavy Shuttle"
			variant
				"Blackbird"
			variant
				"Bounder"
			variant
				"Flivver"
		dialog
			`You boarded the <npc> and arrest its crew. Now you can land back on <origin> to claim your reward.`
	on abort
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Hauling" -= 1
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Security" -= 1
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Hauling" >?= 2
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Security" >?= 2
	on complete
		payment 100000
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Hauling" += 1
		"reputation: MGF: NGK Security" += 1
		"MGF: NGK saboteur arrest job done" += 1
		dialog
			`Armed NGK security personnels arrive to pick up the crew of <npc> you just arrested thanking you and hands you <payment>.`

	word
		"Your passengers ask that you land away from the busy spaceport center. They hand you <payment> and rush out of your ship and away from the spaceport with considerable speed."
		"Your passengers ask that you land away from the busy spaceport center. They hand you <payment> and rush out of your ship and away from the spaceport with considerable speed. Just as you turn around to get back to your ship you hear some shouting from behind. You turn around and see those you just left your ship now kneeling with hands on their head as they're being apprehended by armed security personnels."
		"Your passengers ask that you land away from the busy spaceport center. They hand you <payment> and rush out of your ship and away from the spaceport with considerable speed. #================================Ankulah

phrase "mgf: arrived-without-wreckage dialog"
	word
		`You have reached <planet>, but you left the <npc> behind! Better depart and go pick it up then return here.`

phrase "mgf: wreckage recovery complete"
	word
		`You contact the traffic control as you approach the <planet> then detach the wreckage at the assigned orbit near the station before heading to land. Once landed one of the station crew walks up to you and handed you <payment>.`

phrase "mgf: wreckage assisted"
	word
		`You boarded the wreckage and after a quick scan to analyze the cargo and spot for weak points the crew then begins to perform rudimentary reinforcement where's necessary and prepare for it to dock.`

	description "Defeat a pirate raid on <destination>."
	minor
	repeat
	to offer
		"combat rating" > 100
		random < 10
		"reputation: Independent" > 0
		"reputation: MGF: Ankulah Crew" > 0
	source
		not government "Pirate"
		planet "Ankulah Ship Breaking Station"
	npc evade
		government "Pirate"
		personality hunting target harvests plunders
		fleet "Small Northern Pirates" 3
		fleet "Large Northern Pirates"
	npc
		government "MGF: Ankulah Crew"
		personality hunting staying
		fleet "MGF: Ankulah Guard"
	on offer
		conversation
			`Suddenly you hear raised voices and shouting: "We are under attack by pirates! We need every combat-worthy ship to join the defenses!" The authorities will probably pay you quite well if you assist them, but this could also be an easy way to get yourself killed.`
			choice
				`	(Stay here until the fight is over.)`
					decline
				`	(Join the defense fleet.)`
			`The local Ankulah guard power up their few barely combat-worthy ship preparing to repel the pirate attack. You join them, and take off together...`
				launch
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic pirate fleet battle on visit"
	on complete
		"reputation: Independent" += 1
		"reputation: MGF: Ankulah Crew" += 1
		payment 200000
		dialog phrase "generic pirate attack payment dialog"

	word
		`You help them lift various materials from the ground up to the building they're working on. ` 
		`You picked up prefabricated pieces of bridge up to position and hold it while the workers below join it. `
		`You assist them lifting a prefabricated house around as they're rearranging a village. `
		`You assist in some tear down carrying large chunk of a building away to the dump site. `
		`You helped the port unloading containers off a massive freighter that arrived a few minutes after you did. `
		`Your job was to carry some landfill from a site some distance away as someone figured it'd be faster with a spaceship than a convoy of trucks. `
		`You helped them transporting supplies between the depot and the worksite deep in some inaccessible mountainous area. `
	word
		`After a few hours you finished the job, the foreman thank you and handed you <payment>.`

	cargo "Nuclear Fuel" 20 75
	to offer
		or
			random < 30
			and
				random < 30
				"flagship attribute: radioactive cargo space" > 0
			and
				random < 30
				"ship model: SRC41C Curie" > 0
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "radioactive mining"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes station
		distance 3 10
	to accept
		or
			"flagship attribute: radioactive cargo space" > 0
			"ship model: SRC41C Curie" > 0
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail

	on complete
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload nuclear fuel station"
		payment 780000 680

	name "Nuclear Transport near <system>"
	repeat
	job
	description "A nuclear transport fleet has been spotted near the <system> system. Join in destroying them and return to <planet> for a cut of the loot (<payment>)."
	to offer
		random < 10
		"combat rating" > 150
		"reputation: Pirate" > 0
	source
		government "Pirate"
		attributes "core pirate"
	npc
		government "Pirate"
		personality disables plunders harvests escort
		fleet "Small Core Pirates"
		fleet "Small Core Pirates"
	
	npc kill
		personality heroic staying target
		government "MGF: Core Nuclear Transport"
		system
			distance 1 3
		fleet "MGF: Small Core Nuclear Transport"
		dialog "The merchants have been eliminated. Return to <destination> for your cut of the loot."
	on complete
		payment 250000
		dialog "After counting up the loot from the destroyed merchant fleet, you are given your cut. <payment>"

mission "Nuclear Cargo Theft (Core)"
	name "Convoy near <system>"
	job
	repeat
	description `A nuclear transport fleet has been spotted near the <system> system. A local warlord is interested in having the nuclear cask with Uranium in it from the <npc>. Plunder it and return to <planet> by <day> for payment of <payment>.`
	to offer
		random < 5
		"combat rating" > 3000
		"outfit (flagship installed): Cargo Scanner" > 0
	deadline 20
	source
		government Pirate
		attributes "core pirate"
	npc
		government "MGF: Core Nuclear Transport"
		personality staying heroic target
		system
			not government "Pirate"
			distance 2 2
		fleet "MGF: Small Core Nuclear Transport (Cask Job)"
			
	on visit
		dialog "You land on <planet>, but you don't have the nuclear cask or you do not have the correct cask! Return to the <npc> and bring the correct cargo back to <planet>."
	to complete
		has "outfit (flagship cargo): Nuclear Cask (Uranium)"
	on complete
		outfit "Nuclear Cask (Uranium)" -1
		payment 4500000
		dialog "The warlord's crew come to inspect the cargo before loading it into their truck and hands you <payment>."

#=======================================Sugar

phrase "mgf: unload sugar bag"
	word
		`Once landed you begin the process to bag the sugar and unload it via an elevator on the starboard of your ship to be loaded into waiting trucks. After the last bag was sent down <payment> is transferred into your account.`

mission "MGF: Sugar Transport (to bag) 1"
	name "Bulk Sugar to <planet>"
	description "1000 tons of White Sugar along with <cargo> to bag the cargo when arriving at <destination> by <date>. Payment is <payment>. To accept this job you need flagship capable of carrying bulk sugar and bagging it."
	job
	repeat
	deadline
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "sugar bag" 30
	to offer
		or
			random < 20
			and
				random < 70
				has "outfit (installed): B-type 200 Bulk Sugar Bay"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "farming"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "paradise" "near earth" "urban"
		distance 3 7
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): B-type 200 Bulk Sugar Bay" >= 10 + ( "outfit (installed): White Sugar" / 100 )
	on accept
		outfit "White Sugar" 1000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "White Sugar" -1000
	on complete
		outfit "White Sugar" -1000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload sugar bag"
		payment 95000 275

phrase "mgf: unload wine"
	word
		`You parked your tanker at the wine packaging facility and after signing some paper work you begin unloading the cargo. After the last drop was discharged the facility manager hands you <payment>.`

mission "MGF: Wine Transport (Red Wine 1)"
	name "Bulk Wine to <planet>"
	description "1000 units of Red Wine along with <cargo> to confirm the delivery is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>. To accept this job you need flagship capable of carrying wine."
	job
	repeat
	deadline
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		or
			random < 20
			and
				random < 60
				has "outfit (installed): C-type 100 Wine Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "paradise" "near earth"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "paradise" "near earth"
		distance 3 20
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): C-type 100 Wine Tank" >= 20 + ( "outfit (installed): Red Wine" / 50 ) + ( "outfit (installed): White Wine" / 50 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Rose Wine" / 50 )
	on accept
		outfit "Red Wine" 1000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Red Wine" -1000
	on complete
		outfit "Red Wine" -1000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload wine"
		payment 450000 6500

		attributes "paradise" "near earth"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "paradise" "near earth" "urban"
		distance 3 20
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): C-type 100 Wine Tank" >= 10 + ( "outfit (installed): Red Wine" / 50 ) + ( "outfit (installed): White Wine" / 50 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Rose Wine" / 50 )
	on accept
		outfit "Red Wine" 500
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Red Wine" -500
	on complete
		outfit "Red Wine" -500
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload wine"
		payment 230000 6700

#=======================================Juice

trade
	commodity "Packaged Juice"
		"Bottled Orange Juice"
		"Bottled Apple Juice"
		"Bottled Peach Juice"
		"Bottled Pineapple Juice"
		"Bottled Coconut Water"
		"Canned Orange Juice"
		"Canned Apple Juice"
		"Canned Peach Juice"
		"Canned Pineapple Juice"
		"Canned Coconut Water"

phrase "mgf: juice distribution done"
	word
		`After you landed you look around for a truck painted in white and orange as described by your client and see a person in similarly themed uniform waving at you. After unloading the cargo from the ship and into the truck <payment> is transferred into your account.`

mission "MGF: Juice Distribution [0]"
	name "Juice Distribution to <planet>"
	job
	repeat
	deadline 1 1
	description "Deliver <cargo> to <destination>, to avoid spoilage it must be delivered by <date>. Payment is <payment>."
	cargo "Packaged Juice" 10 3 .12
	to offer
		or
			random < 30
			and
				#Having reefer ship boost offer chance.
				random < 60
				or
					has "flagship attribute: refrigerated space"
					has "ship model: QYG-30r Qazan"
					has "ship model: QYG-70r Tonazqi"
					has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
	source
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes urban
	destination
		distance 2 5
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on complete
		"MGF: Juice Distribution Done" += 1
		payment
		payment 6500
		dialog phrase "mgf: juice distribution done"

mission "MGF: Juice Transport (Orange Juice 1)"
	name "Bulk Juice to <planet>"
	description "800 units of Concentrated Orange Juice along with <cargo> to verify the delivery is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>."
	job
	repeat
	deadline
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		random < 50 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
		has "outfit (installed): C-type 200 Juice Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "farming"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "urban"
		distance 3 20
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): C-type 200 Juice Tank" >= 8 + ( "outfit (installed): Conc. Orange Juice" / 100 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Conc. Apple Juice" / 100 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Conc. Pineapple Juice" / 100 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Conc. Coconut Water" / 100 )
	on accept
		outfit "Conc. Orange Juice" 800
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Conc. Orange Juice" -800
	on complete
		outfit "Conc. Orange Juice" -800
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload juice"
		payment 18000 4000

#=======================================RORO Jobs
trade
	commodity "RORO Cargo" #330 730
		"cars"
		"sports cars"
		"luxury cars"
		"vans"
		"buses"
		"trucks"
		"tractors"
		"semi-trailer trucks"
		"trailers"
		"crane trucks"
		"refrigerated trucks"
		"construction vehicles"
		
phrase "mgf: car shipping complete"
	word
		`You deploy the ramp and the crew begin driving <commodity> off the ship. <payment> is transferred into your account once the last vehicle left your ship.`
		
mission "MGF: Car Shipping 1"
	name "Vehicles to <planet>"
	description "Ship <cargo> to <destination> by <date>. Payment is <payment>."
	job
	repeat
	deadline
	cargo "RORO Cargo" 25 50
	to offer
		random < 40 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
		or
			#If other plugin will add car carrier, having "car carrier" attribute on the ship can allow these jobs to offer as well. Due to limitation only ones on flagship can be used.
			#For car carriers from Mega Freight it will be listed individually so they still works on escorts.
			has "flagship attribute: car carrier"
			has "ship model: LVC-2 Sandura"
			"outfit (installed): MGF: Car Cargo Bay" >= 20
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 2 12
		not attributes "station"
	to accept
		or
			has "flagship attribute: car carrier"
			has "ship model: LVC-2 Sandura"
			"outfit (installed): MGF: Car Cargo Bay" >= 25
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	to complete
		or
			has "flagship attribute: car carrier"
			has "ship model: LVC-2 Sandura"
			"outfit (installed): MGF: Car Cargo Bay" >= 20
	on complete
		dialog phrase "mgf: car shipping complete"
		payment 12000 180

#======================================Livestock

trade
	commodity "Livestock"
		"sheep"
		"cow"
		"goat"
		"pig"
		"chicken"
		
phrase "mgf: livestock transport complete"
	word
		`You deploy the ramp and the crew begin herding the <commodity> off the ship. <payment> is transferred into your account once the last <commodity> left your ship.`
		
mission "MGF: Livestock Transport 1"
	name "Livestock to <planet>"
	description "Export <cargo> to <destination> by <date>. Payment is <payment>. Aborting will result in a fine."
	job
	repeat
	deadline
	cargo "Livestock" 50
	to offer
		or #40% normall or 70% if ranching planet.
			random < 40 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
			and
				random < 70 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
				"flagship planet attribute: ranching" >= 1
		or
			has "flagship attribute: livestock space"
			has "ship model: PL-50 Impavid"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes "farming"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 2 12
		not attributes "station"
	to accept
		or
			has "flagship attribute: livestock space"
			has "ship model: PL-50 Impavid"
		or
			"flagship attribute: livestock space" >= ( 50 + "mgf: current carried livestock" )
			
			#Number of livestock carrier is enough. Condition math is done in int so anything less than 1 will be rounded down.
			#(newLivestock + currentLivestock) / shipCapacity
			"ship model: PL-50 Impavid" >= ( 50 + "mgf: current carried livestock" ) / 300
	on accept
		"mgf: current carried livestock" += 50
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	to complete
		or
			has "flagship attribute: livestock space"
			has "ship model: PL-50 Impavid"
	on abort
		"mgf: current carried livestock" -= 50
		payment -18000 -300
	on complete
		"mgf: current carried livestock" -= 50
		dialog phrase "mgf: livestock transport complete"
		payment 18000 280

mission "MGF: Bulk Livestock Transport 1"
	name "Livestock to <planet>"
	description "Export <cargo> to <destination> by <date>. Payment is <payment>. Aborting will result in a fine."
	job
	repeat
	deadline
	cargo "Livestock" 200
	to offer
		or
			random < 40 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
			and
				random < 60 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
				"flagship planet attribute: ranching" >= 1
		or
			has "flagship attribute: livestock space"
			has "ship model: PL-50 Impavid"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes "farming"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 2 12
		not attributes "station"
	to accept
		or
			has "flagship attribute: livestock space"
			has "ship model: PL-50 Impavid"
		or
			"flagship attribute: livestock space" > ( 200 + "mgf: current carried livestock" )
			
			#Number of livestock carrier is enough. Condition math is done in int so anything less than 1 will be rounded down.
			#(newLivestock + currentLivestock) / shipCapacity
			"ship model: PL-50 Impavid" >= ( 200 + "mgf: current carried livestock" ) / 300
	on accept
		"mgf: current carried livestock" += 200
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	to complete
		or
			has "flagship attribute: livestock space"
			has "ship model: PL-50 Impavid"
	on abort
		"mgf: current carried livestock" -= 200
		payment -32000 -300
	on complete
		"mgf: current carried livestock" -= 200
		dialog phrase "mgf: livestock transport complete"
		payment 32000 265
		
mission "MGF: Bulk Livestock Transport to Paradise 1"
	name "Livestock to <planet>"
	description "Export <cargo> to <destination> by <date>. Payment is <payment>. Aborting will result in a fine."
	job
	repeat
	deadline
	cargo "Livestock" 200
	to offer
		or
			random < 30 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
			and
				random < 60 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
				"flagship planet attribute: ranching" >= 1
		or
			has "flagship attribute: livestock space"
			has "ship model: PL-50 Impavid"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes "farming"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 2 12
		attributes "paradise"
		not attributes "station"
	to accept
		or
			has "flagship attribute: livestock space"
			has "ship model: PL-50 Impavid"
		or
			"flagship attribute: livestock space" > ( 200 + "mgf: current carried livestock" )

			"ship model: PL-50 Impavid" >= ( 200 + "mgf: current carried livestock" ) / 300
	on accept
		"mgf: current carried livestock" += 200
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	to complete
		or
			has "flagship attribute: livestock space"
			has "ship model: PL-50 Impavid"
	on abort
		"mgf: current carried livestock" -= 200
		payment -52000 -400
	on complete
		"mgf: current carried livestock" -= 200
		dialog phrase "mgf: livestock transport complete"
		payment 52000 400

phrase "mgf: refrigerated transport complete"
	word
		`After unloading the last of <commodity>, <payment> is transferred into your account.`
		
mission "MGF: Small Refrigerated Transport 1"
	name "Refrigerated Cargo to <planet>"
	description "Transport <cargo> to <destination> by <date>. Payment is <payment>."
	job
	repeat
	deadline 1 1
	cargo "Refrigerated Food" 5 20
	to offer
		#offer if you have reefer ship, higher chance on planet with fruit export attribute
		or
			random < 50 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
			and
				random < 80 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
				has "flagship planet attribute: fruit export"
		or
			has "flagship attribute: refrigerated space"
			has "ship model: QYG-30r Qazan"
			has "ship model: QYG-70r Tonazqi"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Refrigerated Cargo Bay"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes "farming"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 2 12
	to accept
		or
			has "flagship attribute: refrigerated space"
			has "ship model: QYG-30r Qazan"
			has "ship model: QYG-70r Tonazqi"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Refrigerated Cargo Bay"
		# No checking if there's enough refrigerated space right now, too lazy. Also won't work with random numbers.
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	to complete
		or
			has "flagship attribute: refrigerated space"
			has "ship model: QYG-30r Qazan"
			has "ship model: QYG-70r Tonazqi"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Refrigerated Cargo Bay"
	on complete
		dialog phrase "mgf: refrigerated transport complete"
		payment 18000 350

			has "ship model: QYG-70r Tonazqi"

		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"

	to accept

			has "flagship attribute: frozen space"
			has "ship model: QYG-70r Tonazqi"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Frozen Cargo Bay"

		or

			has "ship model: QYG-70r Tonazqi"

#==============Fishing/ Fish Factory ships
		
phrase "mgf: fishing on visit"
	word
		`You have reached <planet>, but you either haven't visited all the planets yet or your fishing or reefer ship hasn't arrived yet! Better depart and make sure you visit <stopovers> or wait for your escort to arrive.`

phrase "mgf: fishing from origin on visit"
	word
		`You have reached <planet>, but your fishing or reefer ship hasn't arrived yet! Better wait for your escort to arrive.`

phrase "mgf: fishing at stopover"
	word
		`You find a good fishing spot as you approach the planet. After landing for refuelling and post-flight check at the port you then head toward the fishing area. Splashing down near the location you begin to scan for group of fish using your fishfinder sonar and locate a sizeable group to approach and catch. The caught fish were then pulled up into the ship, processed, and stored. Now you can head back to <origin> to deliver the cargo.`

phrase "mgf: fishing at origin"
	word
		`After accepting the job you find a good fishing area then head toward it. Splashing down near the location you begin to scan for group of fish using your fishfinder sonar and locate a sizeable group to approach and catch. The caught fish were then pulled up into the ship, processed, and stored. Now you can head to <destination> to deliver the cargo.`

#todo: more detail about the processing?

mission "MGF: Special Fish Order 1"
	name "Special Order Fish from <planet stopovers>"
	description "A client on <origin> wants <tons> of exotic fish from <planet stopovers> delivered back to <origin> by <date>, they will pay <payment> for it. (Either a fishing ship or reefer ship need to be present for delivery.)"
	job
	repeat
	deadline 0 2
	cargo "(reserved for fish)" 10 50
	to offer
		or
			random < 5
			and
				random < 40 + ( "mgf: fishing experience" / 10 )
				or
					has "outfit (installed): FV-8 Trawler System"
					has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes "rich" "urban"
	stopover
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 2 20
		attributes `fishing`
	to accept
		or
			has "outfit (installed): FV-8 Trawler System"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
		# No checking if there's enough frozen space right now, too lazy. Also won't work with random numbers.
	on stopover
		"mgf: fishing experience" += 1
		#todo: check if fishing ship is present(not necessary as flagship) when it can be done without invalidating the mission if arrived without one.
		dialog phrase "mgf: fishing at stopover"
	on visit
		dialog phrase "mgf: fishing on visit"
	to complete
		or
			has "outfit (installed): FV-8 Trawler System"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
			has "ship model: QYG-30r Qazan"
			has "ship model: QYG-70r Tonazqi"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Refrigerated Cargo Bay"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Frozen Cargo Bay"
	on complete
		dialog
			`You unloaded the fishes you caught from <planet stopovers> and receive your payment of <payment>.`
		payment 520000 880

mission "MGF: Special Fish Order 2"
	name "Special Order Fish from <planet stopovers>"
	description "A client on <origin> wants <tons> of exotic fish from <planet stopovers> delivered back to <origin> by <date>, they will pay <payment> for it. (Either the a fishing ship or reefer ship need to be present for delivery.)"
	job
	repeat
	deadline 0 2
	cargo "(reserved for fish)" 10 100
	to offer
		or
			and
				random < 25 + ( "mgf: fishing experience" / 10 )
				or
					has "outfit (installed): FV-8 Trawler System"
					has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes "rich" "urban"
	stopover
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 2 20
		attributes `fishing`
	to accept
		or
			has "outfit (installed): FV-8 Trawler System"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
		# No checking if there's enough frozen space right now, too lazy. Also won't work with random numbers.
	on stopover
		"mgf: fishing experience" += 1
		dialog phrase "mgf: fishing at stopover"
	on visit
		dialog phrase "mgf: fishing on visit"
	to complete
		or
			has "outfit (installed): FV-8 Trawler System"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
			has "ship model: QYG-30r Qazan"
			has "ship model: QYG-70r Tonazqi"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Refrigerated Cargo Bay"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Frozen Cargo Bay"
			#You can carry fresh fish reefers as well (in fact they're made for this job too), so any reefer is valid for delivery.
	on complete
		dialog
			`You unloaded the fishes you caught from <planet stopovers> and receive your payment of <payment>.`
		payment 520000 980

		"fresh trout"
		"fresh salmon"
		"fresh cod"
		"fresh sardine"
		"fresh mackerel"
		"fresh anchovy"
		"fresh pollock"

		"fresh sunracer salmon"
		"fresh poseidos cod"

mission "MGF: Fishing Delivery 1"
	name "Fresh Fish to <planet>"
	description "Market at <planet> is looking to purchase <cargo> from <origin> for <payment>, fish it then deliver it to <destination> by <date>. (Either a fishing ship or reefer ship need to be present for delivery.)"
	job
	repeat
	deadline 0 3
	cargo "Fresh Fish" 50 160
	to offer
		random < 40 + ( "mgf: fishing experience" / 10 )
		or
			has "outfit (installed): FV-8 Trawler System"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes `fishing`
	stopover
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 2 7
		not attributes `fishing`
	to accept
		or
			has "outfit (installed): FV-8 Trawler System"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
	on accept
		"mgf: fishing experience" += 1
		dialog phrase "mgf: fishing at origin"
			
	on visit
		dialog phrase "mgf: fishing from origin on visit"

	to complete
		or
			has "outfit (installed): FV-8 Trawler System"
			has "ship model: DSSN-S90 Lynchyoseu"
			has "ship model: QYG-30r Qazan"
			has "ship model: QYG-70r Tonazqi"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Refrigerated Cargo Bay"
			has "outfit (installed): MGF: Frozen Cargo Bay"
	on complete
		dialog
			`You unloaded the fishes you caught from <planet stopovers> and receive your payment of <payment>.`
		payment 200000 450

#================================Yacht Carrier

phrase "mgf: yacht transport complete"
	word
		`Arriving on <planet> you land your ship in the water as told by your client as the crew of the ship pack up and head to their yacht. Flooding the yacht bay then opening the bay door soon the yacht begins to drive out. During the process <payment> is transferred into your account.`

mission "MGF: Yacht Transport 1"
	name "Yacht Transport to <planet>"
	description "A rich client want their <cargo> along with its crew of <bunks> to be transported to <destination> by <date>. Payment is <payment>."
	job
	repeat
	deadline 0 4
	passengers 5 12
	cargo "luxury motor yacht" 120 300
	to offer
		random < 20 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
		or
			has "flagship attribute: marine ship space"
			has "ship model: DSSN-C40 Dulumi"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		attributes "rich" "urban"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Neutral" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security"
		distance 2 8
		not attributes station frontier 
	to accept
		or
			has "flagship attribute: marine ship space"
			has "ship model: DSSN-C40 Dulumi"
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	to complete
		or
			has "flagship attribute: marine ship space"
			has "ship model: DSSN-C40 Dulumi"
	on complete
		dialog phrase "mgf: yacht transport complete"
		payment 1220000 550

#======================================Cement

phrase "mgf: unload cement"
	word
		"You dock your ship to the special unloading port and discharge the cargo to the trucks waiting. After the last truck is fully loaded <payment> is transferred into your account."

mission "MGF: Cement Transport 1"
	name "Cement Transport to <planet>"
	description "2000 units of Cement along with <cargo> to verify the batch is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>."
	job
	repeat
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		random < 50 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
		has "outfit (installed): U-type 1k Cement Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing" "mining"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing" "urban"
		distance 3 20
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): U-type 1k Cement Tank" >= 2 + ( "outfit (installed): Cement" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Fly Ash" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Granulated Slag" / 1000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Cement" 2000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Cement" -2000
	on complete
		outfit "Cement" -2000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload cement"
		payment 800000 6500

#===================================Aggregate

phrase "mgf: unload aggregate"
	word
		"You dock your ship to the special unloading port and discharge the cargo to the trucks waiting. After the last truck is fully loaded <payment> is transferred into your account."

trade
	commodity "Aggregate"
		"Flint"
		"Crushed Basalt"
		"Crushed Granite"
		"Crushed Quartz"
		"Slag"
		"Recycled Concrete"

	name "Aggregate Transport to <planet>"
	description "Ship <cargo> to <destination>. Payment is <payment>."
	job
	repeat
	cargo "Aggregate" 200
	to offer
		random < 40 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
		or
			has "ship model: FAd36 Flint"
			has "flagship attribute: aggregate bay"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing" "mining"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing" "urban"
		distance 3 20
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on complete
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload aggregate"

		random < 30 + ( 100 * ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Fast Unloading" * 20 / ( "cargo attractiveness" + 2 ) * 10 ) ) / 10
		or
			has "ship model: FAd36 Flint"
			has "flagship attribute: aggregate bay"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing" "mining"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing" "urban"
		distance 3 20
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on complete
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload aggregate"
		payment 60000 350

#=======================================GAS

#"Lure" job that shows up even if player don't meet the requirement to give example of Gas shipping job.
mission "MGF: Gas Transport (LNG 1)"
	name "Gas Transport to <planet>"
	description "4000 units of Liquid Natural Gas along with <cargo> to confirm the validity is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>. To accept this job you need flagship capable of carrying liquid gas."
	job
	repeat
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		or
			random < 50
			and
				random < 70
				has "outfit (installed): M-type 1k Gas Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing" "oil"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing"
		distance 3 20
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): M-type 1k Gas Tank" >= 2 + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Natural Gas" / 2000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Ethane" / 2000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Hydrogen" / 2000 )
		#Wait for when missions can install outfit in escort.
		#"outfit (installed): M-type 1k Gas Tank" >= 2 + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Natural Gas" / 2000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Ethane" / 2000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Hydrogen" / 2000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Liquid Natural Gas" 4000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Liquid Natural Gas" -4000
	on complete
		outfit "Liquid Natural Gas" -4000
		dialog "You discharge the gas at a special port near the industrial site and receive your payment of <payment>"
		payment 1000000 15000
		
mission "MGF: Gas Transport (LNG 2)"
	name "Gas Transport to <planet>"
	description "4000 units of Liquid Natural Gas along with <cargo> to confirm the validity is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>."
	job
	repeat
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		random < 40
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing" "oil"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing"
		distance 3 20
	on offer
		require "M-type 1k Gas Tank" 2
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): M-type 1k Gas Tank" >= 2 + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Natural Gas" / 2000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Ethane" / 2000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Liquid Hydrogen" / 2000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Liquid Natural Gas" 4000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Liquid Natural Gas" -4000
	on complete
		outfit "Liquid Natural Gas" -4000
		dialog "You discharge the gas at a special port near the industrial site and receive your payment of <payment>"
		payment 1000000 16000

#=======================================Oil

phrase "mgf: unload oil"
	word
		`You parked at a special port near the industrial zone and after signing some paper work the cargo is pumped out of your tank. Halfway through payment of <payment> is transferred into your account.`

mission "MGF: Oil Transport (Crude Oil 1)"
	name "Oil Transport to <planet>"
	description "4000 units of Crude Oil along with <cargo> to verify the batch is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>. To accept this job you need flagship capable of carrying oil."
	job
	repeat
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		or
			random < 50
			and
				random < 70
				has "outfit (installed): B-type 1k Oil Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "oil"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing"
		distance 3 20
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): B-type 1k Oil Tank" >= 4 + ( "outfit (installed): Crude Oil" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Gasoline" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Machine Oil" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Kerosene" / 1000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Crude Oil" 4000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Crude Oil" -4000
	on complete
		outfit "Crude Oil" -4000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload oil"
		payment 1500000 5000

		"outfit (flagship installed): B-type 1k Oil Tank" >= 2 + ( "outfit (installed): Crude Oil" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Gasoline" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Machine Oil" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Kerosene" / 1000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Kerosene" 2000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Kerosene" -2000
	on complete
		outfit "Kerosene" -2000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload oil"
		payment 1000000 8000

	name "Oil Transport to <planet>"

	job

	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		or
			random < 60
			and
				random < 80
				has "outfit (installed): B-type 1k Oil Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "oil"
		not attributes "oil refinery"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "oil refinery"
		not attributes "oil"
		distance 3 20
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): B-type 1k Oil Tank" >= 4 + ( "outfit (installed): Crude Oil" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Gasoline" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Machine Oil" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Kerosene" / 1000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Crude Oil" 4000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Crude Oil" -4000
	on complete
		outfit "Crude Oil" -4000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload oil"
		payment 1500000 4900

#=======================================Bitumen

phrase "mgf: unload bitumen regular"
	word
		`Soon after you landed several tanker truck arrive and park next to the ship's discharge area. You deploy the discharging arms to connect to the tankers and unload the cargo of bitumen. After the last tanker is filled up <payment> is transferred into your account.`

phrase "mgf: unload bitumen urban"
	word
		`You dock your ship at the special port for discharging bitumen and unload the cargo. After all cargo has been unloaded <payment> is transferred into your account.`


mission "MGF: Bitumen Transport (Regular 1)"
	name "Bitumen Transport to <planet>"
	description "4000 units of Bitumen along with <cargo> to verify the batch is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>."
	job
	repeat
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		random < 60
		has "ship model: LAC-4 Lithalsa"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "oil"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		not attributes station
		distance 3 20
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): B-type 1k Bitumen Tank" >= 4 + ( "outfit (installed): Bitumen" / 1000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Bitumen" 4000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Bitumen" -4000
	on abort
		outfit "Bitumen" -4000
	on complete
		outfit "Bitumen" -4000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload bitumen regular"
		payment 500000 11000

mission "MGF: Chemical Transport (Sulfuric 1)"
	name "Chemical Transport to <planet>"
	description "2000 units of Sulfuric Acid along with <cargo> to confirm the validity is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>. To accept this job you need flagship capable of carrying highly corrosive chemical."
	job
	repeat
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		or
			random < 50
			and
				random < 80
				has "outfit (installed): M-type 1k Gas Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing"
		distance 3 20
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): U-type 1k Chemical Tank" >= 2 + ( "outfit (installed): Sulfuric Acid" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Phosphoric Acid" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Methanol" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Ammonia" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Hydrazine" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Diborane" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Chlorine" / 1000 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Hydrochloric Acid" / 1000 )
	on accept
		outfit "Sulfuric Acid" 2000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Sulfuric Acid" -2000
	on complete
		outfit "Sulfuric Acid" -2000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload chemical"
		payment 500000 9000

#==============================Molasses

phrase "mgf: unload molasses"
	word
		`You unload the chemical at a special port and receive your payment of <payment>`

mission "MGF: Molasses Transport (Sugar Cane 1)"
	name "Molasses Transport to <planet>"
	description "2000 units of Sugar Cane Molasses along with <cargo> to confirm the batch is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>. To accept this job you need flagship capable of carrying molasses."
	job
	repeat
	deadline
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		random < 80
		has "outfit (installed): U-type 500 Molasses Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "farming"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing" "urban"
		distance 3 10
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): U-type 500 Molasses Tank" >= 8 + ( "outfit (installed): Sugar Cane Molasses" / 250 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Beet Molasses" / 250 )
	on accept
		outfit "Sugar Cane Molasses" 2000
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "Sugar Cane Molasses" -2000
	on complete
		outfit "Sugar Cane Molasses" -2000
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload molasses"
		payment 220000 11000

mission "MGF: Molasses Transport (Beet 1)"
	name "Molasses Transport to <planet>"
	description "2000 units of Beet Molasses along with <cargo> to confirm the batch is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>. To accept this job you need flagship capable of carrying molasses."
	job
	repeat
	deadline
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "paper works" 1
	to offer
		random < 70
		has "outfit (installed): U-type 500 Molasses Tank"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "farming"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing" "urban"
		distance 3 10
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): U-type 500 Molasses Tank" >= 8 + ( "outfit (installed): Sugar Cane Molasses" / 250 ) + ( "outfit (installed): Beet Molasses" / 250 )

#======================Garbage

phrase "mgf: unload garbage"
	word
		`You unload the garbage at the `
	word
		`processing plant`
		`dump site`
		`recycling plant`
	word
		` and receive your payment of <payment>.`

mission "MGF: Garbage Transport (Garbage 1)"
	name "Garbage Transport to <planet>"
	description "250 units of Garbage along with <cargo> to verify the shipment is required to be shipped to <destination>. Payment is <payment>. To accept this job you need flagship capable of compacting garbage."
	job
	repeat
	deadline
	#So Multiplier works.
	cargo "notes" 1
	to offer
		random < 70
		has "outfit (installed): B-type 500 Garbage Bay"
	source
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "farming" "frontier" "mining"
		not attributes "urban"
	destination
		government "Republic" "Syndicate" "Free Worlds" "Independent" "MGF: NGK Hauling" "MGF: NGK Security" "SpaceCrate"
		attributes "factory" "manufacturing"
		not attributes "station"
		distance 3 10
	to accept
		"outfit (flagship installed): B-type 500 Garbage Bay" >= 1 + ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Garbage" / 250 )
	on accept
		outfit "MGF: Garbage" 250
	on visit
		dialog phrase "generic cargo on visit"
	on fail
		outfit "MGF: Garbage" -250
	on complete
		outfit "MGF: Garbage" -250
		dialog phrase "mgf: unload garbage"
		payment 25000 6250

mission "MGF: Garbage Transport (Garbage 2)"

		"outfit (flagship installed): B-type 500 Garbage Bay" >= 1 + ( "outfit (installed): MGF: Garbage" / 250 )

		fail
	on offer
		
		payment 8600
		conversation
			`Shortly after landing you found some Hai walking up to you asking about the uniquely designed rollercoaster on your ship and if they could ride it, of course they've prepared payment for the ride. Looking around you estimated that you could get at least 2000 credits here, possibly much more if you leave it open for longer.`
			choice
				`	(Yes.)`
				`	(Not now.)`
					defer
				`	(Never.)`
					decline
			action
				payment 8600
			`	You agreed to let them take a ride. At the end of the day you've made 8600 credits in total profit from offering rollercoaster ride to the Hai.`
				accept

#==============================Mining

mission "MGF: Mine Titanium Tiny"
	name "Mine Titanium"
	description "Someone wants a delivery of 15 tons of raw Titanium, mine it and return to <origin> before <date> for payment of <payment>."
	repeat
	job
	deadline 30
	source
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent"
		not attributes "uninhabited"
	to offer
		or
			and
				random < 15
				or
					"ships: Interceptor" > 0
					"ships: Light Warship" > 0
					"ships: Utility" > 0
			random < 7

	on complete
		outfit "Titanium" -15
		payment 52500 #40
		dialog `You delivered 15 tons of Titanium and received a payment of <payment>`

mission "MGF: Mine Titanium Small"
	name "Mine Titanium"
	description "Someone wants a delivery of 30 tons of raw Titanium, mine it and return to <origin> before <date> for payment of <payment>."
	repeat
	job
	deadline 30
	source
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent"
		not attributes "uninhabited"
	to offer
		or
			and
				random < 7
				or
					"ships: Interceptor" > 0
					"ships: Light Warship" > 0
					"ships: Utility" > 0
			random < 4

	on complete
		outfit "Titanium" -30
		payment 108750 # 45 percent more
		dialog `You delivered 30 tons of Titanium and received a payment of <payment>`

mission "MGF: Mine Titanium Medium"
	name "Mine Titanium"
	description "Someone wants a delivery of 90 tons of raw Titanium, mine it and return to <origin> before <date> for payment of <payment>."
	repeat
	job
	deadline 30
	source
		government "Republic" "Free Worlds" "Syndicate" "Neutral" "Independent"
		not attributes "uninhabited"
	to offer
		or
			and
				random < 4
				or
					"ships: Interceptor" > 0
					"ships: Light Warship" > 0
					"ships: Utility" > 0
			random < 2
		"cargo space" >= 40

	on complete
		outfit "Titanium" -90
		payment 337500 #50
		dialog `You delivered 90 tons of Titanium and received a payment of <payment>`
